<h3 data-section-id="huuihu" data-start="451" data-end="463">已确定的核心规则</h3>
<ul data-start="465" data-end="807">
<li data-section-id="161qf5q" data-start="465" data-end="510">
<p data-start="467" data-end="510">Restaurant Setup Pro 是第一个餐饮家具行业版本，不是系统最终边界。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="qmk32m" data-start="511" data-end="554">
<p data-start="513" data-end="554">AI 是整个系统的 <strong data-start="523" data-end="541">Business Brain</strong>，不是单独的 AI 模块。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1l26a8e" data-start="555" data-end="582">
<p data-start="557" data-end="582"><strong data-start="557" data-end="582">Lead 与 Customer 永远分开。</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="6k8xd0" data-start="583" data-end="612">
<p data-start="585" data-end="612">AI 只分析、建议、生成内容，不自动修改正式业务数据。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="zi4pkw" data-start="613" data-end="642">
<p data-start="615" data-end="642">每次 AI 调用都必须经过 Cost Control。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="j83x1g" data-start="643" data-end="672">
<p data-start="645" data-end="672">不开发复杂 ERP，只保留生产、运输和售后的关键状态。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1tbfiai" data-start="673" data-end="710">
<p data-start="675" data-end="710">开发方式从 Module01、Module02 改为完整业务流程开发。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="o81n8b" data-start="711" data-end="747">
<p data-start="713" data-end="747">每条流程必须经过：开发 → 测试 → 业务验证 → 再进入下一流程。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="10simgg" data-start="748" data-end="807">
<p data-start="750" data-end="807">Opportunity Intelligence 已完成约 90%，后续以检查、补漏、接入新流程为主，不从头重做。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="chbcs4" data-start="809" data-end="820">下一步正确操作</h3>
<p data-start="822" data-end="832">请在这个对话中上传：</p>
<ul data-start="834" data-end="978">
<li data-section-id="ciga26" data-start="834" data-end="913">
<p data-start="836" data-end="913"><strong data-start="836" data-end="913">Restaurant Setup Pro AI Sales OS V5.3 Lite Development Specification V1.0</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="odj3ty" data-start="914" data-end="978">
<p data-start="916" data-end="978"><strong data-start="916" data-end="978">Opportunity Intelligence V3.2 CRM Workflow Refactor Report</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="980" data-end="1043">《AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0》目前还没有正式完成，下一步将由我们在这个对话中整理。</p>
<p data-start="1045" data-end="1079">文件上传后，先不直接给 Codex 新开发指令，而是先完成三项工作：</p>
<ol data-start="1081" data-end="1226">
<li data-section-id="4l16ju" data-start="1081" data-end="1134">
<p data-start="1084" data-end="1134">对照 Project Brief、V5.3 技术规范和 V3.2 已开发报告，确认现有系统真实状态。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1jbmsru" data-start="1135" data-end="1161">
<p data-start="1138" data-end="1161">找出旧设计与新业务原则之间的冲突、重复和缺失。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="17jalg2" data-start="1162" data-end="1226">
<p data-start="1165" data-end="1226">正式整理 <strong data-start="1170" data-end="1209">AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</strong>，确定完整业务流程和后续开发顺序。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="1228" data-end="1239">预计后续主开发顺序为：</p>
<p data-start="1241" data-end="1476"><strong data-start="1241" data-end="1476">Knowledge Foundation → Opportunity Discovery Execution → Lead Qualification → Lead to Customer → Customer Requirement → Product Matching → Quote / PI → Order Confirmation → Production / Shipping Tracking → After Sales → AI Learning</strong></p>
<p data-start="1478" data-end="1535" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">这条主线确定后，再给 Codex 一段一段执行，避免继续出现开发内容反复修改、模块之间无法形成完整业务闭环的问题。</p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] <ol data-start="44" data-end="212">
<li data-section-id="9d2ahm" data-start="44" data-end="126">
<p data-start="47" data-end="126"><strong data-start="47" data-end="85">Restaurant Setup Pro - Development</strong><br data-start="85" data-end="88">

负责新的总体架构、业务蓝图、后续开发规划和Codex指令。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="214" data-end="341">移动方法：在左侧对话列表找到对应对话，点击“…” → <strong data-start="241" data-end="268">Move to project / 移动到项目</strong> → 选择原来的项目。对话移入后，会继承该项目中的项目指令和文件上下文。<span class="" data-state="closed"><span class="ms-1 inline-flex max-w-full items-center select-none relative top-[-0.094rem] translate-y-0.5 animate-[show_150ms_ease-in]" data-testid="webpage-citation-pill" style="width: 108px;"><a href="https://help.openai.com/en/articles/10169521-projects-in-chatgpt?utm_source=chatgpt.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener" alt="https://help.openai.com/en/articles/10169521-projects-in-chatgpt?utm_source=chatgpt.com" class="flex overflow-hidden rounded-xl text-[9px] font-medium h-4.5 pe-2 ps-1 transition-colors duration-150 ease-in-out text-token-text-secondary! bg-[#F4F4F4]! dark:bg-[#303030]! select-none" style="max-width: 108px;"><span class="relative start-0 bottom-0 flex h-full w-full items-center"><span class="flex h-4 w-full items-center justify-between overflow-hidden" style="opacity: 1; transform: none;"><span class="flex min-w-0 flex-1 items-center gap-1"><span class="inline-flex shrink-0 items-center justify-center overflow-hidden rounded-full"><img alt="" width="128" height="128" class="h-3 w-3 rounded-full" src="./AI_SALES_OS_BUSINESS_BLUEPRINT_V1.0_files/favicons"></span><span class="max-w-[15ch] grow truncate overflow-hidden text-center">OpenAI Help Center</span></span></span></span></a></span></span></p>
<h3 data-section-id="vldos8" data-start="343" data-end="353">项目名称建议</h3>
<p data-start="355" data-end="366">如果原来的项目现在叫：</p>
<p data-start="368" data-end="392"><strong data-start="368" data-end="392">Restaurant Setup Pro</strong></p>
<p data-start="394" data-end="402">建议以后改名为：</p>
<p data-start="404" data-end="430"><strong data-start="404" data-end="430">Restaurant AI Sales OS</strong></p>
<p data-start="432" data-end="441">因为现在已经明确：</p>
<ul data-start="443" data-end="540">
<li data-section-id="86e2ys" data-start="443" data-end="473">
<p data-start="445" data-end="473">Restaurant AI Sales OS 是母系统；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="j386eo" data-start="474" data-end="510">
<p data-start="476" data-end="510">Restaurant Setup Pro 是第一个餐饮家具行业版本；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="yni2ql" data-start="511" data-end="540">
<p data-start="513" data-end="540">以后还会扩展酒店家具、办公家具、建材、机械设备等版本。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="x3sq1z" data-start="542" data-end="552">项目内的结构</h3>
<p data-start="554" data-end="571">同一个项目中保留两个主要对话即可：</p>
<ul data-start="573" data-end="682">
<li data-section-id="ydzfz0" data-start="573" data-end="627">
<p data-start="575" data-end="627"><strong data-start="575" data-end="613">Restaurant Setup Pro - Development</strong>：旧系统开发记录和已完成功能</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1pq5xd6" data-start="628" data-end="682">
<p data-start="630" data-end="682"><strong data-start="630" data-end="670">Restaurant AI Sales OS - Development</strong>：从现在开始的主开发对话</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="684" data-end="729">不要删除旧对话，也不要把所有短视频、图片生成、市场营销等无关对话都移进去。这个项目只保留：</p>
<ul data-start="731" data-end="792">
<li data-section-id="1anq0dl" data-start="731" data-end="740">
<p data-start="733" data-end="740">产品与业务架构</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1oxdqm6" data-start="741" data-end="747">
<p data-start="743" data-end="747">开发规范</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="5qwwbw" data-start="748" data-end="757">
<p data-start="750" data-end="757">Codex开发</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ntq9ll" data-start="758" data-end="764">
<p data-start="760" data-end="764">测试报告</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1rnf8tt" data-start="765" data-end="774">
<p data-start="767" data-end="774">数据库和API</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="6ykg1a" data-start="775" data-end="792">
<p data-start="777" data-end="792">AI Sales OS相关文件</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="794" data-end="860" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">所以，<strong data-start="797" data-end="860" data-is-last-node="">这两个开发对话都加入原来的开发项目；今后主要在当前这个 Restaurant AI Sales OS 对话中继续推进。</strong></p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] justify-start"><div aria-label="回复操作" class="touch:-me-2 touch:-ms-3.5 -ms-2.5 -me-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-y-4 <p data-start="32" data-end="41">现在按这个顺序做：</p>
<h3 data-section-id="1dul15s" data-start="43" data-end="63">第一步：把两个文件上传到当前对话</h3>
<p data-start="65" data-end="69">请上传：</p>
<ol data-start="71" data-end="217">
<li data-section-id="klza3g" data-start="71" data-end="151">
<p data-start="74" data-end="151"><strong data-start="74" data-end="151">Restaurant Setup Pro AI Sales OS V5.3 Lite Development Specification V1.0</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="irt8lz" data-start="152" data-end="217">
<p data-start="155" data-end="217" class="" style=""><strong data-start="155" data-end="217">Opportunity Intelligence V3.2 CRM Workflow Refactor Report</strong></p>
</li>
</ol>
<p data-start="219" data-end="258">如果还有最新的开发完成报告、系统检查报告，也可以一起上传，但先以上面两个为准。</p>
<h3 data-section-id="1mp5orh" data-start="260" data-end="278">第二步：我做一次“现状对齐”</h3>
<p data-start="280" data-end="290">我会对照三部分内容：</p>
<ul data-start="292" data-end="378">
<li data-section-id="1bww26m" data-start="292" data-end="323">
<p data-start="294" data-end="323">你刚刚确定的 <strong data-start="301" data-end="323">Project Brief V1.0</strong></p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="nm8eve" data-start="324" data-end="340">
<p data-start="326" data-end="340">V5.3 Lite 技术规范</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="sxnu02" data-start="341" data-end="378">
<p data-start="343" data-end="378">Opportunity Intelligence V3.2 已开发内容</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="380" data-end="385">然后输出：</p>
<ul data-start="387" data-end="463">
<li data-section-id="hlr2er" data-start="387" data-end="398">
<p data-start="389" data-end="398">已经真正完成的功能</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="tkp3mq" data-start="399" data-end="409">
<p data-start="401" data-end="409">还没有完成的功能</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="2inp1v" data-start="410" data-end="419">
<p data-start="412" data-end="419">重复开发的部分</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1gz1ulx" data-start="420" data-end="434">
<p data-start="422" data-end="434">与最新业务原则冲突的地方</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1k7jiih" data-start="435" data-end="450">
<p data-start="437" data-end="450">必须保留、修改、删除的内容</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="159yk7u" data-start="451" data-end="463">
<p data-start="453" data-end="463">下一阶段正确开发入口</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="ajodry" data-start="465" data-end="482">第三步：整理正式的业务蓝图</h3>
<p data-start="484" data-end="487">完成：</p>
<p data-start="489" data-end="528"><strong data-start="489" data-end="528">AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</strong></p>
<p data-start="530" data-end="538">这份蓝图会明确：</p>
<ul data-start="540" data-end="660">
<li data-section-id="1d9l75p" data-start="540" data-end="548">
<p data-start="542" data-end="548">系统用户是谁</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1v1f11k" data-start="549" data-end="572">
<p data-start="551" data-end="572">从企业知识导入到成交、出货、售后的完整流程</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="5xai9r" data-start="573" data-end="594">
<p data-start="575" data-end="594">Lead 与 Customer 的边界</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ets168" data-start="595" data-end="609">
<p data-start="597" data-end="609">每个流程中 AI 做什么</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="25gwol" data-start="610" data-end="618">
<p data-start="612" data-end="618">人工确认什么</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1rzminx" data-start="619" data-end="628">
<p data-start="621" data-end="628">数据保存在哪里</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ecqjr9" data-start="629" data-end="641">
<p data-start="631" data-end="641">每一步如何进入下一步</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1aa1ymk" data-start="642" data-end="660">
<p data-start="644" data-end="660">哪些内容属于第一版，哪些暂缓开发</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="1oozvj3" data-start="662" data-end="681">第四步：确定第一个完整开发流程</h3>
<p data-start="683" data-end="730">不会立刻把 Knowledge Center 全部做完，而是先选一个可以真正跑通的闭环，例如：</p>
<p data-start="732" data-end="804"><strong data-start="732" data-end="804">企业知识导入 → AI生成搜索策略 → 创建Search Task → 获取Lead → AI评分 → 人工确认 → 转Customer</strong></p>
<p data-start="806" data-end="818">这个闭环跑通后，再进入：</p>
<p data-start="820" data-end="876"><strong data-start="820" data-end="876">Customer Requirement → Product Matching → Quote → PI</strong></p>
<h3 data-section-id="jd5opw" data-start="878" data-end="900">第五步：再生成 Codex 开发指令</h3>
<p data-start="902" data-end="921">后续每次给 Codex 的内容都采用：</p>
<ul data-start="923" data-end="1009">
<li data-section-id="14v7wvr" data-start="923" data-end="931">
<p data-start="925" data-end="931">本次业务目标</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1bkzo9g" data-start="932" data-end="940">
<p data-start="934" data-end="940">当前系统现状</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ojav75" data-start="941" data-end="949">
<p data-start="943" data-end="949">允许修改范围</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="tr793b" data-start="950" data-end="958">
<p data-start="952" data-end="958">禁止破坏范围</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ahuhah" data-start="959" data-end="966">
<p data-start="961" data-end="966">数据库变更</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="e45th" data-start="967" data-end="973">
<p data-start="969" data-end="973">页面流程</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1e5dc7q" data-start="974" data-end="982">
<p data-start="976" data-end="982">AI调用规则</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ntpqrb" data-start="983" data-end="989">
<p data-start="985" data-end="989">测试标准</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1ycjo37" data-start="990" data-end="996">
<p data-start="992" data-end="996">验收标准</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="6khaxz" data-start="997" data-end="1009">
<p data-start="999" data-end="1009">GitHub同步要求</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1011" data-end="1045">这样避免 Codex 只完成页面或单个功能，却没有形成完整业务流程。</p>

<h2 data-section-id="1p9kf8" data-start="235" data-end="244">一、对齐结论</h2>
<h3 data-section-id="7m5m0n" data-start="246" data-end="257">已经一致的内容</h3>
<p data-start="259" data-end="269">以下原则不需要改变：</p>
<ul data-start="271" data-end="678">
<li data-section-id="gdr8z" data-start="271" data-end="407">
<p data-start="273" data-end="407">不推翻、重建现有系统，继续复用 Product Library、Product Intelligence、Price Engine、Quote Builder、PI Builder、Opportunity Intelligence 和 AI Cost Control。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="5jcnrg" data-start="408" data-end="446">
<p data-start="410" data-end="446">AI默认只提供分析、建议和草稿，不能自动修改价格、产品、客户等正式数据。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ct7rzv" data-start="447" data-end="475">
<p data-start="449" data-end="475">所有付费AI调用必须经过 Cost Control。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ybhzoo" data-start="476" data-end="502">
<p data-start="478" data-end="502">AI生成的客户沟通、报价和PI内容必须人工确认。</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1svhvkv" data-start="503" data-end="678">
<p data-start="505" data-end="539">Lead 与 Customer 已经在V3.2中完成概念和页面分离：</p>
<p data-start="545" data-end="678"><strong data-start="545" data-end="640">Search Task → Search Result → Lead Pool → Lead Detail → Convert to Customer → Customers CRM</strong>。<span class="relative inline-flex items-center select-none" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_6u8_" data-state="closed"><button type="button" class="ms-1 relative flex h-[25px] select-none items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-xl px-2 text-[10px] leading-[13px] corner-superellipse/1.1 text-token-text-secondary! hover:text-token-text-primary! hover:bg-token-bg-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary dark:hover:bg-token-bg-secondary bg-[#f4f4f4] "><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="h-[16px] w-[16px] object-contain text-token-text-primary! flex-none icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fec7759e.svg#554074" fill="currentColor"></use></svg><p class="not-prose mt-0! mb-0! flex-auto truncate">V5.3-OPPORTUNITY-INTELLIGENCE-V…</p></button></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 data-section-id="uoga8i" data-start="680" data-end="691">需要修正的内容</h3>
<h4 data-start="693" data-end="709">1. 开发方式需要更新</h4>
<p data-start="711" data-end="721">旧V5.3规范按照：</p>
<p data-start="723" data-end="764"><strong data-start="723" data-end="764">Phase 0 → Phase 1 → Phase 2 → Phase 3</strong></p>
<p data-start="766" data-end="806">推进。<span class="relative inline-flex items-center select-none" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_6ud_" data-state="closed"><button type="button" class="ms-1 relative flex h-[25px] select-none items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-xl px-2 text-[10px] leading-[13px] corner-superellipse/1.1 text-token-text-secondary! hover:text-token-text-primary! hover:bg-token-bg-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary dark:hover:bg-token-bg-secondary bg-[#f4f4f4] "><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="h-[16px] w-[16px] object-contain text-token-text-primary! flex-none icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fec7759e.svg#554074" fill="currentColor"></use></svg><p class="not-prose mt-0! mb-0! flex-auto truncate">V5.3-DEVELOPMENT-SPECIFICATION-…</p></button></span></p>
<p data-start="808" data-end="813">现在改为：</p>
<p data-start="815" data-end="851"><strong data-start="815" data-end="851">一个完整业务流程 → 测试 → 实际业务验证 → 再进入下一流程</strong></p>
<p data-start="853" data-end="884">原来的Phase编号可以保留为技术分类，但不能再决定开发顺序。</p>
<h4 data-start="886" data-end="912">2. Customer数据归属需要重新明确</h4>
<p data-start="914" data-end="1016">旧规范把“Customer and opportunity data”统一归入 Opportunity Intelligence。<span class="relative inline-flex items-center select-none" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_6uh_" data-state="closed"><button type="button" class="ms-1 relative flex h-[25px] select-none items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-xl px-2 text-[10px] leading-[13px] corner-superellipse/1.1 text-token-text-secondary! hover:text-token-text-primary! hover:bg-token-bg-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary dark:hover:bg-token-bg-secondary bg-[#f4f4f4] "><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="h-[16px] w-[16px] object-contain text-token-text-primary! flex-none icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fec7759e.svg#554074" fill="currentColor"></use></svg><p class="not-prose mt-0! mb-0! flex-auto truncate">V5.3-DEVELOPMENT-SPECIFICATION-…</p></button></span></p>
<p data-start="1018" data-end="1026">新规则必须拆开：</p>
<div class="TyagGW_tableContainer"><div tabindex="-1" class="group TyagGW_tableWrapper flex flex-col-reverse w-fit"><table data-start="1028" data-end="1325" class="w-fit <p data-start="1327" data-end="1379">Lead转成Customer以后，保留Lead来源和历史，但不能继续把Customer当成Lead管理。</p>
<h4 data-start="1381" data-end="1427">3. “Opportunity Intelligence完成约90%”需要准确理解</h4>
<p data-start="1429" data-end="1440">目前已经完成的主要是：</p>
<ul data-start="1442" data-end="1572">
<li data-section-id="7xuycn" data-start="1442" data-end="1460">
<p data-start="1444" data-end="1460">AI Discovery页面基础</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="17lst57" data-start="1461" data-end="1474">
<p data-start="1463" data-end="1474">Search Task</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="15jksb3" data-start="1475" data-end="1490">
<p data-start="1477" data-end="1490">Search Result</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="m5gdjs" data-start="1491" data-end="1502">
<p data-start="1493" data-end="1502">Lead Pool</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="uhhqc5" data-start="1503" data-end="1516">
<p data-start="1505" data-end="1516">Lead Detail</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="sr1uvm" data-start="1517" data-end="1534">
<p data-start="1519" data-end="1534">Lead → Customer</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1mnf3j9" data-start="1535" data-end="1552">
<p data-start="1537" data-end="1552">Customers CRM入口</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="zp0r43" data-start="1553" data-end="1572">
<p data-start="1555" data-end="1572">AI评分、证据、产品匹配等展示基础</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1574" data-end="1587">但是V3.2报告明确说明：</p>
<ul data-start="1589" data-end="1739">
<li data-section-id="12q4jeg" data-start="1589" data-end="1604">
<p data-start="1591" data-end="1604">没有新增外部搜索执行能力；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="cuv6cb" data-start="1605" data-end="1617">
<p data-start="1607" data-end="1617">没有新增API集成；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="kanazo" data-start="1618" data-end="1645">
<p data-start="1620" data-end="1645">没有正式Lead Activity Log数据表；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="71buld" data-start="1646" data-end="1678">
<p data-start="1648" data-end="1678">Activity History只是根据现有时间和状态生成；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="16k471m" data-start="1679" data-end="1739">
<p data-start="1681" data-end="1739">V3.2主要完成的是页面、命名和流程重构。<span class="relative inline-flex items-center select-none" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_6uk_" data-state="closed"><button type="button" class="ms-1 relative flex h-[25px] select-none items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-xl px-2 text-[10px] leading-[13px] corner-superellipse/1.1 text-token-text-secondary! hover:text-token-text-primary! hover:bg-token-bg-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary dark:hover:bg-token-bg-secondary bg-[#f4f4f4] "><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="h-[16px] w-[16px] object-contain text-token-text-primary! flex-none icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fec7759e.svg#554074" fill="currentColor"></use></svg><p class="not-prose mt-0! mb-0! flex-auto truncate">V5.3-OPPORTUNITY-INTELLIGENCE-V…</p></button></span></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="1741" data-end="1751">因此更准确的说法是：</p>
<blockquote data-start="1753" data-end="1884">
<p data-start="1755" data-end="1884"><strong data-start="1755" data-end="1884">Opportunity Intelligence的内部页面和Lead工作流基础大部分完成，但真正自动调用Google Maps、Yellow Pages、Apollo、网站和社交平台搜索客户的Search Execution Engine还没有完成。</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<h4 data-start="1886" data-end="1919">4. AI Business Brain不能先做成空架构</h4>
<p data-start="1921" data-end="1989">旧规范原计划先开发独立的 AI Business Brain。<span class="relative inline-flex items-center select-none" type="button" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="radix-_r_6un_" data-state="closed"><button type="button" class="ms-1 relative flex h-[25px] select-none items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-xl px-2 text-[10px] leading-[13px] corner-superellipse/1.1 text-token-text-secondary! hover:text-token-text-primary! hover:bg-token-bg-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary dark:hover:bg-token-bg-secondary bg-[#f4f4f4] "><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="h-[16px] w-[16px] object-contain text-token-text-primary! flex-none icon-sm"><use href="/cdn/assets/sprites-core-fec7759e.svg#554074" fill="currentColor"></use></svg><p class="not-prose mt-0! mb-0! flex-auto truncate">V5.3-DEVELOPMENT-SPECIFICATION-…</p></button></span></p>
<p data-start="1991" data-end="1999">现在应该调整为：</p>
<blockquote data-start="2001" data-end="2059">
<p data-start="2003" data-end="2059">AI Business Brain在具体业务流程中逐步建立，而不是先开发一个庞大、抽象、暂时无法使用的AI中枢。</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-start="2061" data-end="2120">第一个落地流程中先让AI能够读取企业知识、生成搜索策略、分析搜索结果；以后再逐步增加报价、PI、生产、运输和学习能力。</p>
<h2 data-section-id="8bk6i9" data-start="2122" data-end="2142">二、现在不要让Codex继续写代码</h2>
<p data-start="2144" data-end="2154">当前缺少的是正式的：</p>
<h1 data-section-id="o04say" data-start="2156" data-end="2193">AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</h1>
<p data-start="2195" data-end="2252">这份文件将作为Project Brief与技术规范之间的桥梁，解决“业务怎么运行”和“下一步到底开发什么”的问题。</p>
<p data-start="2254" data-end="2262">它需要正式确定：</p>
<ol data-start="2264" data-end="2460">
<li data-section-id="qyc6ey" data-start="2264" data-end="2275">
<p data-start="2267" data-end="2275">系统角色和权限；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="x8scda" data-start="2276" data-end="2304">
<p data-start="2279" data-end="2304">AI Knowledge Center的数据结构；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1f7q1ud" data-start="2305" data-end="2336">
<p data-start="2308" data-end="2336">从Knowledge到After Sales的完整流程；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="dcuq2s" data-start="2337" data-end="2362">
<p data-start="2340" data-end="2362">Lead与Customer的状态和转换条件；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="6ohdft" data-start="2363" data-end="2382">
<p data-start="2366" data-end="2382">每一步AI做什么、人工确认什么；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="18qjmmq" data-start="2383" data-end="2396">
<p data-start="2386" data-end="2396">每类数据的唯一来源；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="qccyuh" data-start="2397" data-end="2420">
<p data-start="2400" data-end="2420">AI Cost Control触发规则；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ge0y3m" data-start="2421" data-end="2440">
<p data-start="2424" data-end="2440">第一版必须开发和暂不开发的范围；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="5uv3z6" data-start="2441" data-end="2460">
<p data-start="2444" data-end="2460">后续按照业务流程执行的开发路线。</p>
</li>
</ol>
<h2 data-section-id="f3l59p" data-start="2462" data-end="2481">三、第一条应该开发的完整业务流程</h2>
<p data-start="2483" data-end="2500">蓝图完成后，第一条开发流程应当是：</p>
<p data-start="2502" data-end="2675"><strong data-start="2502" data-end="2675">AI Knowledge Center → Search Strategy → Search Task → Search Execution → Search Results → Lead Pool → AI Qualification → Lead Detail → Human Review → Convert to Customer</strong></p>
<p data-start="2677" data-end="2682">其中包括：</p>
<ul data-start="2684" data-end="2840">
<li data-section-id="16yfz7j" data-start="2684" data-end="2706">
<p data-start="2686" data-end="2706">AI读取产品、公司、历史客户和价格规则；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1l7v9fq" data-start="2707" data-end="2734">
<p data-start="2709" data-end="2734">AI生成目标国家、客户类型、搜索关键词和平台建议；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="ixp1v5" data-start="2735" data-end="2748">
<p data-start="2737" data-end="2748">销售人员确认搜索任务；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="jsqpnt" data-start="2749" data-end="2766">
<p data-start="2751" data-end="2766">系统调用经过批准的搜索API；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="yx32pp" data-start="2767" data-end="2796">
<p data-start="2769" data-end="2796">搜索结果进入Lead Pool，而不是直接进入CRM；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1qibw94" data-start="2797" data-end="2819">
<p data-start="2799" data-end="2819">AI提供评分、购买信号、证据和产品匹配；</p>
</li>
<li data-section-id="1qf5189" data-start="2820" data-end="2840">
<p data-start="2822" data-end="2840">人工确认后才能转成Customer。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="2842" data-end="2858">这条流程跑通以后，再进入第二条：</p>
<p data-start="2860" data-end="2940"><strong data-start="2860" data-end="2940">Customer Requirement → Product Matching → Quote → PI → Customer Confirmation</strong></p>
<p data-start="2942" data-end="3023" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">现在你不需要再上传其他文件，也暂时不要给Codex新指令。下一项工作就是正式整理 <strong data-start="2983" data-end="3022">AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</strong>。</p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] justify-start"><div aria-label="回复操作" class="touch:-me-2 touch:-ms-3.5 -ms-2.5 -me-1 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-y-4 p-1 var(--spacing)); --writing-block-editor-pb: calc(16 * var(--spacing)); --writing-block-editor-pl: calc(20 * var(--spacing));"><div class="outline-none data-[writing-block-fullscreen-editor]:min-h-[75vh] ProseMirror markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full min-h-6 break-words focus:outline-none" data-writing-block-fullscreen-editor-region="true" data-writing-block-fullscreen-editor-layout="inline" contenteditable="true" aria-disabled="false" dir="auto" translate="no"><h1><span>AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</span></h1><p><strong><span>项目名称：</span></strong><span> Restaurant AI Sales OS</span><br><strong><span>首个行业版本：</span></strong><span> Restaurant Setup Pro — Restaurant Furniture</span><br><strong><span>文件类型：</span></strong><span> Business Blueprint</span><br><strong><span>版本：</span></strong><span> V1.0</span><br><strong><span>状态：</span></strong><span> 项目业务蓝图基准文件</span><br><strong><span>日期：</span></strong><span> 2026年7月11日</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>1. 文件目的</span></h2><p><span>本文件用于定义Restaurant AI Sales OS的业务定位、完整销售流程、数据边界、AI职责、人工职责和后续开发顺序。</span></p><p><span>本文件不是单一模块开发说明，也不直接授权Codex修改代码。</span></p><p><span>它位于以下文件之间：</span></p><p><strong><span>Project Brief V1.0</span></strong><br><span>决定产品方向和最高业务原则。</span></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>AI Sales OS Business Blueprint V1.0</span></strong><br><span>决定业务如何完整运行。</span></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>V5.3 Lite Development Specification V1.0</span></strong><br><span>决定数据库、API、页面、权限和技术实施规则。</span></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>具体业务流程开发指令</span></strong><br><span>授权Codex实施某一条经过确认的完整流程。</span></p><p><span>当旧开发计划与本业务蓝图冲突时，优先遵循：</span></p><ol data-spread="false" start="1"><li><p><span>用户最新明确决定；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Project Brief V1.0；</span></p></li><li><p><span>本Business Blueprint V1.0；</span></p></li><li><p><span>V5.3 Lite Development Specification；</span></p></li><li><p><span>历史模块文档和开发报告。</span></p></li></ol><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>2. 产品定位</span></h2><p><span>Restaurant AI Sales OS是面向B2B企业的AI Sales Operating System。</span></p><p><span>系统不是传统CRM，也不是完整ERP。</span></p><p><span>系统的核心目标是帮助企业完成：</span></p><p><strong><span>学习企业知识</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>发现高价值销售机会</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>筛选和管理潜在客户</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>协助销售沟通、推荐产品和生成报价</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>推动客户确认PI和成交</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>记录生产、运输和售后关键节点</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>学习成功与失败经验</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>优化下一轮获客和成交</span></strong></p><p><span>Restaurant Setup Pro是第一个行业版本，主要服务餐饮家具和商业餐饮空间产品供应企业。</span></p><p><span>未来系统应能够扩展到：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>酒店家具；</span></p></li><li><p><span>办公家具；</span></p></li><li><p><span>建材；</span></p></li><li><p><span>商业设备；</span></p></li><li><p><span>机械设备；</span></p></li><li><p><span>其他需要主动开发客户、产品匹配、报价和项目跟进的B2B行业。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>3. 系统最高原则</span></h2><h3><span>3.1 AI是Business Brain</span></h3><p><span>AI不是一个独立页面或附加模块。</span></p><p><span>AI应贯穿：</span></p><p><strong><span>Knowledge → Discovery → Lead → Customer → Requirement → Quote → PI → Production → Shipping → After Sales → Learning</span></strong></p><p><span>AI在不同阶段使用相同的企业知识和客户上下文，避免每个功能建立独立、重复、互不相通的AI能力。</span></p><h3><span>3.2 业务流程优先</span></h3><p><span>开发不再以Module01、Module02或单独页面为主要顺序。</span></p><p><span>每次开发必须对应一条可以操作、测试和验收的业务流程。</span></p><p><span>例如：</span></p><p><strong><span>导入公司知识 → AI生成搜索策略 → 创建搜索任务 → 执行搜索 → 产生Lead → AI评分 → 人工确认 → 转为Customer</span></strong></p><p><span>只有一条流程完成开发、测试和业务验证后，才能进入下一条流程。</span></p><h3><span>3.3 保留现有系统</span></h3><p><span>不得推翻或重新开发已经存在的基础功能。</span></p><p><span>必须优先复用：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Product Library；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Foundation；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Knowledge Engine；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Price Engine；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Product Import；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Opportunity Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Quote Builder；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI Builder；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>现有权限和Debug基础。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>3.4 AI只建议，人工确认</span></h3><p><span>AI可以：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>分析；</span></p></li><li><p><span>推荐；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生成草稿；</span></p></li><li><p><span>解释；</span></p></li><li><p><span>评分；</span></p></li><li><p><span>提醒；</span></p></li><li><p><span>发现异常。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI不能未经人工确认：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>修改正式产品数据；</span></p></li><li><p><span>修改成本或销售价格；</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建正式Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>发送邮件或WhatsApp；</span></p></li><li><p><span>发送报价或PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>修改订单状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>修改生产、运输或售后结果；</span></p></li><li><p><span>删除业务记录。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>3.5 Lead与Customer永久分离</span></h3><p><span>Lead是尚未正式进入销售跟进的潜在客户。</span></p><p><span>Customer是经过人工确认、正式进入销售流程的客户。</span></p><p><span>Lead转为Customer后：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>原Lead记录保留；</span></p></li><li><p><span>来源、搜索证据和AI分析保留；</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建独立Customer记录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>后续报价、PI、生产和售后挂在Customer下；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer不会因为没有成交而自动退回Lead Pool。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>4. 系统主要用户</span></h2><h3><span>4.1 Administrator</span></h3><p><span>负责：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>公司基本设置；</span></p></li><li><p><span>用户和权限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Provider设置；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI预算和Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索Connector和API设置；</span></p></li><li><p><span>系统日志；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数据安全；</span></p></li><li><p><span>业务规则审批。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>4.2 Business Owner / Sales Manager</span></h3><p><span>负责：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>确认目标国家和客户类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>确认利润和报价规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>审核搜索策略；</span></p></li><li><p><span>查看高价值Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>分配销售人员；</span></p></li><li><p><span>审核重要报价和PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>查看销售结果和AI学习报告。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>4.3 Sales User</span></h3><p><span>负责：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>查看和筛选Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>人工确认Lead转Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>记录客户需求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>使用AI生成沟通内容；</span></p></li><li><p><span>选择和确认产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建报价和PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>更新跟进状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>记录成交或失败原因。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>4.4 Product / Pricing Manager</span></h3><p><span>负责：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>产品资料；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品分类；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品规格和变体；</span></p></li><li><p><span>供应商成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>包装、MOQ和交期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>价格规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>利润要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品适用场景；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品知识审批。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>4.5 Operations User</span></h3><p><span>负责更新：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Production Started；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Production Finished；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Shipping；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Delivered；</span></p></li><li><p><span>After Sales。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>第一版不需要复杂生产计划、仓库管理或供应商采购系统。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>5. 完整业务生命周期</span></h2><p><span>系统主业务流程为：</span></p><h3><span>Stage 1：Knowledge</span></h3><p><span>企业导入和维护：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>公司；</span></p></li><li><p><span>工厂；</span></p></li><li><p><span>价格；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>历史客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交案例；</span></p></li><li><p><span>销售规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>失败经验。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI将这些内容组织为可调用的Business Knowledge。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 2：Discovery Strategy</span></h3><p><span>AI根据企业知识生成：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>目标国家；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标城市；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标客户类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>企业规模；</span></p></li><li><p><span>开店年限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>扩店、翻新或采购信号；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索关键词；</span></p></li><li><p><span>推荐平台；</span></p></li><li><p><span>排除条件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索优先级；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计调用成本。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>人工确认后创建Search Task。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 3：Search Execution</span></h3><p><span>系统根据已确认的Search Task调用获批的Connector或API。</span></p><p><span>可能包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Google Maps；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Yellow Pages；</span></p></li><li><p><span>行业协会；</span></p></li><li><p><span>商业目录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>政府企业注册；</span></p></li><li><p><span>企业网站；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Facebook；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Instagram；</span></p></li><li><p><span>LinkedIn；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Apollo；</span></p></li><li><p><span>其他当地商业信息平台。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>搜索结果首先进入Search Results，不直接创建Customer。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 4：Lead Qualification</span></h3><p><span>系统完成：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>数据标准化；</span></p></li><li><p><span>重复检测；</span></p></li><li><p><span>网站和联系方式整理；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户类型识别；</span></p></li><li><p><span>购买信号识别；</span></p></li><li><p><span>机会评分；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品初步匹配；</span></p></li><li><p><span>证据保存；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI推荐下一步。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>符合基本条件的结果进入Lead Pool。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 5：Lead Review</span></h3><p><span>销售人员在Lead Detail中查看：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>AI Summary；</span></p></li><li><p><span>公司信息；</span></p></li><li><p><span>来源；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Website；</span></p></li><li><p><span>联系方式；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer Evidence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Opportunity Score；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Purchase Potential；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Matching；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Recommendation；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Activity History；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数据更新时间。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>销售人员可以：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>更新Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>保留Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Discard；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Convert to Customer。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Stage 6：Customer CRM</span></h3><p><span>Lead经人工确认后转换为Customer。</span></p><p><span>Customer CRM只保留销售所需的关键内容：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>公司；</span></p></li><li><p><span>联系人；</span></p></li><li><p><span>国家和地区；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>来源Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>负责人；</span></p></li><li><p><span>当前销售阶段；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户需求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>沟通记录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>下一步行动；</span></p></li><li><p><span>报价；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交或失败结果。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>系统不开发传统CRM中大量低价值字段和复杂配置。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 7：Customer Requirement</span></h3><p><span>销售人员记录：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>需要的产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>项目类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>项目地点；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数量；</span></p></li><li><p><span>尺寸；</span></p></li><li><p><span>材质；</span></p></li><li><p><span>颜色；</span></p></li><li><p><span>风格；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预算；</span></p></li><li><p><span>交付时间；</span></p></li><li><p><span>运输要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>定制要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户文件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>尚未确认的问题。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI可以整理客户邮件、WhatsApp、图纸、图片、表格和其他文件中的需求，但必须由销售人员确认后写入正式Requirement。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 8：Product Matching</span></h3><p><span>AI根据：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Customer Requirement；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Library；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品适用场景；</span></p></li><li><p><span>价格范围；</span></p></li><li><p><span>MOQ；</span></p></li><li><p><span>包装；</span></p></li><li><p><span>交期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>利润要求；</span></p></li></ul><p><span>生成产品推荐方案。</span></p><p><span>每项推荐必须提供：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>推荐产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>推荐原因；</span></p></li><li><p><span>匹配程度；</span></p></li><li><p><span>价格或成本风险；</span></p></li><li><p><span>缺失信息；</span></p></li><li><p><span>替代产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>需要人工确认的内容。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI推荐不直接修改Product Library，也不自动加入正式报价。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 9：Quote</span></h3><p><span>销售人员选择产品并创建Quote。</span></p><p><span>Quote Builder负责：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数量；</span></p></li><li><p><span>单价；</span></p></li><li><p><span>折扣；</span></p></li><li><p><span>运费；</span></p></li><li><p><span>税费；</span></p></li><li><p><span>其他费用；</span></p></li><li><p><span>汇率；</span></p></li><li><p><span>利润；</span></p></li><li><p><span>总金额。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>Product Price Engine是成本、参考价格和价格计算规则的唯一来源。</span></p><p><span>AI可以：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>解释价格；</span></p></li><li><p><span>发现低利润；</span></p></li><li><p><span>检查遗漏；</span></p></li><li><p><span>推荐替代产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生成报价说明；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生成客户沟通草稿。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI不能静默改变价格。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 10：PI</span></h3><p><span>客户基本接受报价后，由PI Builder生成正式PI。</span></p><p><span>PI应包含：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Seller；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Buyer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI Number；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品图片；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品描述；</span></p></li><li><p><span>尺寸；</span></p></li><li><p><span>材质和颜色；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数量；</span></p></li><li><p><span>单价；</span></p></li><li><p><span>金额；</span></p></li><li><p><span>包装；</span></p></li><li><p><span>交期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>付款条件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>运输条件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>备注；</span></p></li><li><p><span>总金额；</span></p></li><li><p><span>双方确认信息。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI可以检查：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>产品与报价是否一致；</span></p></li><li><p><span>图片是否缺失；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数量和金额是否异常；</span></p></li><li><p><span>付款和运输条款是否完整；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户要求是否遗漏；</span></p></li><li><p><span>文字表述是否清楚。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>正式发送前必须人工确认。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 11：Confirmed</span></h3><p><span>当客户确认PI或满足企业设定的成交条件后，Customer进入Confirmed。</span></p><p><span>系统记录：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Confirmed PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>确认日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交金额；</span></p></li><li><p><span>付款状态摘要；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计交期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>负责人；</span></p></li><li><p><span>关键备注。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>系统第一版不开发复杂财务和应收账款模块。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 12：Production Tracking</span></h3><p><span>系统只记录关键节点：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Production Started；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Production Finished。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>允许保存：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>开始日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计完成日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>实际完成日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>状态备注；</span></p></li><li><p><span>相关文件或图片；</span></p></li><li><p><span>异常说明。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>不开发：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>BOM生产拆单；</span></p></li><li><p><span>工序管理；</span></p></li><li><p><span>员工排产；</span></p></li><li><p><span>原材料库存；</span></p></li><li><p><span>供应商采购；</span></p></li><li><p><span>车间ERP。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Stage 13：Shipping</span></h3><p><span>系统记录：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Ready to Ship；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Shipping；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Delivered。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>允许保存：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>运输方式；</span></p></li><li><p><span>出运日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计到达日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>实际到达日期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>物流单号；</span></p></li><li><p><span>集装箱号；</span></p></li><li><p><span>文件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>异常；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户通知记录。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>不开发完整物流管理平台。</span></p><h3><span>Stage 14：After Sales</span></h3><p><span>系统记录：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>客户是否收到产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否有质量问题；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否缺件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否需要补发；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户满意度；</span></p></li><li><p><span>售后处理结果；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否可能复购；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否可能扩店；</span></p></li><li><p><span>下一次跟进日期。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Stage 15：Learning</span></h3><p><span>项目完成后，AI整理：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Lead来自哪个平台；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪类搜索关键词有效；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪类客户评分准确；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户购买了什么；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交金额；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交周期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>为什么成交；</span></p></li><li><p><span>为什么报价被接受；</span></p></li><li><p><span>为什么客户失败；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪些产品更容易成交；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪些价格区间有效；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪些沟通方式有效；</span></p></li><li><p><span>哪些证据与成交关系较强。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI只形成Learning Recommendation。</span></p><p><span>重要规则、搜索标准、评分权重和价格策略仍需人工批准后才能生效。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>6. AI Knowledge Center</span></h2><p><span>AI Knowledge Center是系统第一层，不是普通文件库。</span></p><p><span>它负责为Discovery、Qualification、Product Matching、Quote、PI和Learning提供统一上下文。</span></p><h3><span>6.1 Product Knowledge</span></h3><p><span>包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Product ID；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品名称；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品分类；</span></p></li><li><p><span>图片；</span></p></li><li><p><span>描述；</span></p></li><li><p><span>尺寸；</span></p></li><li><p><span>材质；</span></p></li><li><p><span>颜色；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品变体；</span></p></li><li><p><span>MOQ；</span></p></li><li><p><span>包装；</span></p></li><li><p><span>重量和体积；</span></p></li><li><p><span>交期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>供应商；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>参考销售价；</span></p></li><li><p><span>标签；</span></p></li><li><p><span>应用场景；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>可定制内容；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不可实现内容；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品优势；</span></p></li><li><p><span>常见客户问题；</span></p></li><li><p><span>相关案例。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>正式产品数据继续由Product Library、Product Foundation和Product Price Engine管理。</span></p><p><span>Knowledge Center读取和组织这些数据，不建立重复产品主档。</span></p><h3><span>6.2 Company Knowledge</span></h3><p><span>包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>公司介绍；</span></p></li><li><p><span>品牌介绍；</span></p></li><li><p><span>工厂介绍；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成立时间；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生产能力；</span></p></li><li><p><span>主要产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>服务范围；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标市场；</span></p></li><li><p><span>目标客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>公司优势；</span></p></li><li><p><span>认证；</span></p></li><li><p><span>案例；</span></p></li><li><p><span>交付能力；</span></p></li><li><p><span>可以做什么；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不能做什么；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不应向客户承诺什么；</span></p></li><li><p><span>标准沟通语气。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>6.3 Customer Knowledge</span></h3><p><span>包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>历史Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>已转换Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>未成交客户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>国家；</span></p></li><li><p><span>行业；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户规模；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交金额；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交周期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>来源；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交原因；</span></p></li><li><p><span>失败原因；</span></p></li><li><p><span>复购情况；</span></p></li><li><p><span>售后情况。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>6.4 Pricing Knowledge</span></h3><p><span>包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>目标毛利率；</span></p></li><li><p><span>最低毛利率；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不同客户类型价格规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不同国家价格规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>汇率规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>MOQ影响；</span></p></li><li><p><span>包装影响；</span></p></li><li><p><span>运输费用处理；</span></p></li><li><p><span>定制费用规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>折扣审批规则；</span></p></li><li><p><span>特殊项目审批规则。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>成本和确定性计算必须保留在Product Price Engine中。</span></p><h3><span>6.5 Knowledge状态</span></h3><p><span>每条知识应支持：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Draft；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Active；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Outdated；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Archived；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Needs Review。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI默认优先使用Active知识。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>7. Discovery与Lead数据边界</span></h2><h3><span>Search Task</span></h3><p><span>代表一项经过人工确认的搜索任务。</span></p><p><span>保存：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>目标市场；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索平台；</span></p></li><li><p><span>关键词；</span></p></li><li><p><span>排除条件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索范围；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计结果数量；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>执行状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建人；</span></p></li><li><p><span>审批人。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Search Result</span></h3><p><span>代表Connector或API返回的一条原始或标准化搜索结果。</span></p><p><span>它可能不符合Lead条件。</span></p><h3><span>Lead</span></h3><p><span>代表具有一定潜在价值、可以进入人工审查的销售机会。</span></p><p><span>Lead不是Customer。</span></p><h3><span>Customer</span></h3><p><span>代表经过人工确认并正式进入销售跟进的企业或个人客户。</span></p><h3><span>转换规则</span></h3><p><span>只有Lead Detail允许执行Convert to Customer。</span></p><p><span>转换时：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>保留Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>保存转换时间；</span></p></li><li><p><span>保存转换人员；</span></p></li><li><p><span>创建Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>建立Lead和Customer关联；</span></p></li><li><p><span>将关键公司和联系人信息复制到Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不复制无意义的临时AI字段；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不删除搜索证据。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>8. Customer CRM设计原则</span></h2><p><span>CRM必须简单。</span></p><p><span>一次普通状态更新应尽量在30秒内完成。</span></p><p><span>Customer CRM核心阶段为：</span></p><p><strong><span>Customer Requirement</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Quotation / PI Discussion</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Confirmed</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Production Started</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Production Finished</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Shipping</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Delivered</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Completed</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>After Sales</span></strong></p><p><span>Lead不属于Customer CRM阶段。</span></p><p><span>系统允许根据未来业务验证增加少量必要状态，但不得变成复杂、难维护的传统CRM。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>9. AI Business Brain职责</span></h2><p><span>AI Business Brain不是单独保存全部业务数据的数据库。</span></p><p><span>它是一个共享的AI调用和业务上下文协调层。</span></p><p><span>主要职责：</span></p><ol data-spread="false" start="1"><li><p><span>确认当前业务对象；</span></p></li><li><p><span>读取用户权限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>读取相关Knowledge；</span></p></li><li><p><span>读取Lead、Customer、Requirement、Quote或PI上下文；</span></p></li><li><p><span>选择合适的AI能力；</span></p></li><li><p><span>检查Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生成结构化建议；</span></p></li><li><p><span>保存AI执行日志；</span></p></li><li><p><span>等待人工确认；</span></p></li><li><p><span>将确认结果交给正式业务模块处理。</span></p></li></ol><p><span>AI Business Brain不直接拥有：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Product主数据；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer主数据；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Quote正式数据；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI正式数据；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成本和价格主数据。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>10. AI Cost Control</span></h2><p><span>所有付费AI调用必须经过统一Cost Control。</span></p><p><span>每次调用至少记录：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>功能名称；</span></p></li><li><p><span>业务对象；</span></p></li><li><p><span>用户；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Provider；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Model；</span></p></li><li><p><span>输入Token；</span></p></li><li><p><span>输出Token；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>实际成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>执行时间；</span></p></li><li><p><span>结果状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否使用缓存；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否人工确认。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>单次调用</span></h3><p><span>低成本、用户主动触发的单条分析，可以按照已批准规则直接执行。</span></p><h3><span>批量调用</span></h3><p><span>批量搜索、批量网站分析、批量评分、批量生成内容前，必须显示：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>预计处理数量；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计API调用次数；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预计成本；</span></p></li><li><p><span>预算上限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>停止条件。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>用户确认后才能执行。</span></p><h3><span>Fallback</span></h3><p><span>系统必须保留：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Mock Provider；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Rules Provider；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Cache；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Provider Switch；</span></p></li><li><p><span>失败重试限制。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>11. Evidence原则</span></h2><p><span>所有重要AI判断必须尽量提供Evidence。</span></p><p><span>Evidence可以来自：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Website；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Google Maps；</span></p></li><li><p><span>商业目录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>企业注册信息；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Facebook；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Instagram；</span></p></li><li><p><span>LinkedIn；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Apollo；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户文件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>历史沟通；</span></p></li><li><p><span>系统业务记录。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>Evidence应保存：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>来源类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>来源地址或引用；</span></p></li><li><p><span>抓取时间；</span></p></li><li><p><span>摘要；</span></p></li><li><p><span>支持的判断；</span></p></li><li><p><span>可信度；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否过期。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>AI不能只给出“这个客户很有价值”，而不说明依据。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>12. AI Learning Loop</span></h2><p><span>Learning分为三层。</span></p><h3><span>Level 1：记录结果</span></h3><p><span>系统保存：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>搜索；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead；</span></p></li><li><p><span>转换；</span></p></li><li><p><span>报价；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交；</span></p></li><li><p><span>失败；</span></p></li><li><p><span>售后。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Level 2：AI分析</span></h3><p><span>AI发现：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>高价值来源；</span></p></li><li><p><span>无效来源；</span></p></li><li><p><span>高转化客户类型；</span></p></li><li><p><span>高转化产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交周期；</span></p></li><li><p><span>常见失败原因；</span></p></li><li><p><span>有效沟通方式；</span></p></li><li><p><span>评分偏差。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Level 3：人工批准优化</span></h3><p><span>AI提出修改建议，例如：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>增加某类搜索关键词；</span></p></li><li><p><span>降低某类Lead评分；</span></p></li><li><p><span>提高某种购买信号权重；</span></p></li><li><p><span>调整推荐产品；</span></p></li><li><p><span>修改沟通模板；</span></p></li><li><p><span>更新知识；</span></p></li><li><p><span>更新目标客户定义。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>只有人工批准后，建议才能变成新的正式规则。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>13. 数据唯一来源</span></h2><table><tbody><tr><th><span>业务数据</span></th><th><span>Source of Truth</span></th></tr><tr><td><span>产品主数据</span></td><td><span>Product Library / Product Foundation</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>产品知识</span></td><td><span>Product Knowledge Engine</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>产品图片和属性</span></td><td><span>Product Library / Product Foundation</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>产品成本和参考价格</span></td><td><span>Product Price Engine</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>公司知识</span></td><td><span>AI Knowledge Center</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>搜索任务</span></td><td><span>Discovery / Search Tasks</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>搜索原始结果</span></td><td><span>Search Results</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Lead</span></td><td><span>Lead Pool / Opportunity Intelligence</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Customer</span></td><td><span>Customers CRM</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>Customer Requirement</span></td><td><span>Customer CRM</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>AI分析和建议</span></td><td><span>AI Analysis Records</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>正式Quote</span></td><td><span>Quote Builder</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>正式PI</span></td><td><span>PI Builder</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>生产状态</span></td><td><span>Production Tracking</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>运输状态</span></td><td><span>Shipping Tracking</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>售后状态</span></td><td><span>After Sales</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>AI调用和成本</span></td><td><span>AI Cost Control</span></td></tr><tr><td><span>AI学习建议</span></td><td><span>Learning Recommendations</span></td></tr></tbody></table><p><span>任何新流程都不得绕过这些Source of Truth另建重复主数据。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>14. 第一版范围</span></h2><h3><span>第一版必须具备</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>AI Knowledge Center基础；</span></p></li><li><p><span>公司知识；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品知识调用；</span><br><span>-目标客户定义；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Search Strategy生成；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Search Task确认；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Connector-ready Search Execution；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Search Results；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead Pool；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead Detail；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Qualification；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Evidence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Matching；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead人工转Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>简单Customer CRM；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer Requirement；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Quote；</span></p></li><li><p><span>PI；</span></p></li><li><p><span>生产关键状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>运输关键状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>售后记录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI执行日志；</span></p></li><li><p><span>人工确认；</span></p></li><li><p><span>基础Learning Recommendation。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>第一版暂不开发</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>完整ERP；</span></p></li><li><p><span>仓库；</span></p></li><li><p><span>库存；</span></p></li><li><p><span>采购订单；</span></p></li><li><p><span>供应商协同平台；</span></p></li><li><p><span>复杂生产排程；</span></p></li><li><p><span>完整财务系统；</span></p></li><li><p><span>自动发送邮件；</span></p></li><li><p><span>自动发送WhatsApp；</span></p></li><li><p><span>无限制网页抓取；</span></p></li><li><p><span>无人工审核的客户沟通；</span></p></li><li><p><span>SaaS自动计费；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Marketplace；</span></p></li><li><p><span>多行业模板市场；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI自动修改核心业务规则。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>15. 开发路线</span></h2><p><span>后续不再按照旧Phase顺序直接开发，而按照以下完整业务流程推进。</span></p><h3><span>Workflow 1：Knowledge to Qualified Lead</span></h3><p><strong><span>Knowledge Center</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>AI Search Strategy</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Human Approval</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Search Task</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Search Execution</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Search Results</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Lead Pool</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>AI Qualification + Evidence + Product Matching</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Human Review</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Convert to Customer</span></strong></p><p><span>完成标准：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>企业知识能够被AI读取；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI能够生成有依据的搜索策略；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索任务必须人工确认；</span></p></li><li><p><span>搜索结果不会直接进入Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI评分具有Evidence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>人工可以Convert或Discard；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead历史完整保留；</span></p></li><li><p><span>所有付费调用进入Cost Control。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Workflow 2：Customer Requirement to Quote and PI</span></h3><p><strong><span>Customer</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Requirement Capture</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>AI Requirement Summary</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Human Confirmation</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Product Matching</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Quote Draft</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Price and Margin Review</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Customer Discussion</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>PI Draft</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Human Approval</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Confirmed</span></strong></p><p><span>完成标准：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>客户需求结构化；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI识别缺失信息；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品推荐来自正式Product Library；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成本和价格来自Price Engine；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Quote与PI数据一致；</span></p></li><li><p><span>产品图片不缺失；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI不能自动发送；</span></p></li><li><p><span>所有正式内容经过人工确认。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Workflow 3：Confirmed Order to Delivery</span></h3><p><strong><span>Confirmed</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Production Started</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Production Finished</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Shipping</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Delivered</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Completed</span></strong></p><p><span>完成标准：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>销售可以快速更新关键状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>状态变化有时间和人员记录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>支持上传必要文件和图片；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不引入复杂ERP；</span></p></li><li><p><span>客户页面可以查看项目当前状态。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Workflow 4：After Sales to Learning</span></h3><p><strong><span>After Sales</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Outcome Capture</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Deal / Loss Analysis</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Learning Recommendation</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Human Approval</span></strong></p><p><span>↓</span></p><p><strong><span>Knowledge / Search Rule Improvement</span></strong></p><p><span>完成标准：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>成交和失败原因可记录；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI能分析来源、客户、产品和成交结果；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI只能提出建议；</span></p></li><li><p><span>正式规则必须人工审批；</span></p></li><li><p><span>下一轮Discovery可以使用批准后的经验。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>16. 每条开发指令的强制结构</span></h2><p><span>以后每次交给Codex的开发任务必须包含：</span></p><ol data-spread="false" start="1"><li><p><span>业务流程名称；</span></p></li><li><p><span>本次业务目标；</span></p></li><li><p><span>用户操作起点；</span></p></li><li><p><span>用户操作终点；</span></p></li><li><p><span>现有功能复用；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数据Source of Truth；</span></p></li><li><p><span>允许修改的文件和范围；</span></p></li><li><p><span>禁止修改的功能；</span></p></li><li><p><span>数据库变更；</span></p></li><li><p><span>API变更；</span></p></li><li><p><span>页面变更；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI输入和输出；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>权限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>人工确认点；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Evidence要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>测试要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>回归测试；</span></p></li><li><p><span>文档要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Git和GitHub同步要求；</span></p></li><li><p><span>已知限制；</span></p></li><li><p><span>明确停止条件。</span></p></li></ol><p><span>Codex完成当前任务后，不得自动进入下一条流程。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>17. 测试和业务验证</span></h2><p><span>每条流程必须经过四层验收。</span></p><h3><span>第一层：技术测试</span></h3><p><span>至少包括：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>npm test；</span></p></li><li><p><span>API health；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Debug database；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Syntax check；</span></p></li><li><p><span>权限测试；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Cost Control测试；</span></p></li><li><p><span>现有功能回归测试。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>第二层：页面测试</span></h3><p><span>确认：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>页面可以正常进入；</span></p></li><li><p><span>按钮清楚；</span></p></li><li><p><span>状态清楚；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead和Customer不混淆；</span></p></li><li><p><span>错误提示清楚；</span></p></li><li><p><span>不出现重复入口；</span></p></li><li><p><span>业务员操作简单。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>第三层：完整业务流程测试</span></h3><p><span>使用一条真实或接近真实的数据，从流程起点走到流程终点。</span></p><p><span>不得只测试单个API或单个页面。</span></p><h3><span>第四层：业务验证</span></h3><p><span>由实际业务人员确认：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>是否符合真实工作；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否减少人工操作；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否容易理解；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否在30秒内完成常规录入；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI建议是否有价值；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否存在错误自动化风险；</span></p></li><li><p><span>是否值得进入下一条流程。</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>18. 当前系统判断</span></h2><p><span>截至V3.2：</span></p><p><span>已经具备：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>AI Discovery入口；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Search Tasks；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Search Results；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead Pool；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead Detail；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customers入口；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead转Customer；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Summary展示；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Evidence展示；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Matching展示；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Update Intelligence；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Convert和Discard；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Priority View基础。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>尚未完整具备：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>正式AI Knowledge Center；</span></p></li><li><p><span>基于企业知识生成Search Strategy；</span></p></li><li><p><span>实际外部Search Execution Engine；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Connector统一管理；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Google Maps等真实数据执行；</span></p></li><li><p><span>完整Lead Activity Log；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer Requirement完整流程；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Customer到Quote、PI的端到端流程；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Production、Shipping、After Sales闭环；</span></p></li><li><p><span>成交与失败Learning Loop。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>因此，Opportunity Intelligence不能重新开发，但需要作为Workflow 1的中后段被复用和补齐。</span></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>19. 下一阶段正式入口</span></h2><p><span>下一阶段不是重新开发Opportunity Intelligence，也不是直接开发复杂AI Business Brain。</span></p><p><span>正式入口是：</span></p><h1><span>Workflow 1 — Knowledge to Qualified Lead</span></h1><p><span>第一步先完成：</span></p><p><strong><span>AI Knowledge Center Foundation</span></strong></p><p><span>需要定义：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Company Knowledge；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Product Knowledge调用；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Target Customer Profile；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Pricing和Margin规则读取；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Existing Customer Learning输入；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Knowledge状态；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Knowledge审核；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Context Builder；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Cost Control；</span></p></li><li><p><span>权限；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Debug可见性。</span></p></li></ul><p><span>随后接入：</span></p><p><strong><span>Search Strategy → Search Task → Search Execution → Lead Pool → AI Qualification → Convert to Customer</span></strong></p><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>20. Blueprint确认原则</span></h2><p><span>本Business Blueprint批准后：</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>原V5.3技术规范继续有效；</span></p></li><li><p><span>旧Phase编号仅作为技术分类；</span></p></li><li><p><span>后续开发改为业务流程驱动；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Lead与Customer永久分离；</span></p></li><li><p><span>Opportunity Intelligence现有成果继续复用；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI Knowledge Center成为下一阶段开发入口；</span></p></li><li><p><span>每条流程单独出Codex指令；</span></p></li><li><p><span>每条流程完成测试和业务验证后才能继续；</span></p></li><li><p><span>AI始终受人工确认、权限和Cost Control约束。</span></p></li></ul></div></div></div><div data-writing-block-fullscreen-shell-border="true" aria-hidden="true" class="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 rounded-[inherit] z-[2] [box-shadow:inset_0_0_0_1px_var(--oai-wb-border)] group-hover/writing-block-surface:[box-shadow:inset_0_0_0_1px_var(--oai-wb-border-hover)]"></div></div></div>
<p data-start="14718" data-end="14820" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">这份蓝图已经可以作为后续开发的业务基准。下一步应制作 <strong data-start="14745" data-end="14767">Workflow 1现有系统差距清单</strong>，再据此形成第一段Codex开发指令，而不是立即让Codex直接开发整个Knowledge Center。</p></div></div></div></div><div class="z-0 flex min-h-[46px] justify-start"><div aria-label="回复操作" class="touch:-me-2 <h2 data-section-id="cldw2s" data-start="534" data-end="545">这两份文件的作用</h2>
<p data-start="547" data-end="591"><strong data-start="547" data-end="591"><code data-start="549" data-end="589">AI_SALES_OS_BUSINESS_BLUEPRINT_V1.0.md</code></strong></p>

</li>

</li>

</li>

<p data-start="687" data-end="753"><strong data-start="687" data-end="753"><code data-start="689" data-end="751">WORKFLOW_01_KNOWLEDGE_TO_QUALIFIED_LEAD_GAP_ANALYSIS_V1.0.md</code></strong></p>

are helping the user get started with ChatGPT Work during the ChatGPT onboarding experience. Make this feel like a welcoming, hands-on first session: help the user accomplish something real, make good defaults, and let each useful result teach them what ChatGPT Work can do. ChatGPT Work is especially useful for larger, multi-step, creative, connected, or recurring tasks.\\n\\nPersonalize from high-confidence context already available about the user, such as their current request, interests, work, preferences, prior conversations, connected tools, or ongoing projects. Do not surface sensitive or surprising details. Make confident choices when the intent is clear instead of repeatedly asking broad questions like “What do you want to do?”\\n\\nKeep the experience warm, concise, and outcome-focused. Do not make it feel like a form, wizard, setup checklist, or product tour. Avoid long roadmaps, numbered steps, and large menus. Prefer doing useful work, showing a concrete result, and then offering one natural next step only when it follows from the result. Let the result demonstrate the capability without narrating the product.\\n\\nKeep thinking/progress updates process-only. Do not draft or preview user-facing answer content there. Put substantive content only in the final response. When using $answers-ask-user-input, its brief lead-in and widget are the final response for that turn; do not preview them first.\\n\\nAsk only when a real choice would materially improve the result or a safety-relevant ambiguity blocks progress. Ask one focused question at a time. Whenever you ask the user any question during this onboarding experience, use the bundled $answers-ask-user-input skill from @Demos rather than asking in ordinary prose. This includes confirmations, preference questions, provider or source choices, corrections, approvals, and open-ended feedback. After invoking it, stop and wait for the answer. If context is sufficient, proceed without asking. Ask User Input changes only the interaction UI and never replaces an exact preview or required confirmation for a write, send, share, or automation.\\n\\nWhen the user's requested task needs an app or connector, first check for a verified relevant connection and use it when available. If no relevant connection exists and the user already named a provider, help connect that provider directly. If the provider is genuinely unclear, briefly explain what you can help connect, then invoke $answers-ask-user-input with one focused provider question and only the concrete providers available for that task. For example: Google Calendar or Microsoft Outlook Calendar for calendar work; Gmail or Microsoft Outlook for email; Slack or Microsoft Teams for messaging; Google Drive, Microsoft OneDrive, SharePoint, or Box for files. After the user chooses, help connect that provider, wait until the connection succeeds, and then continue the original task. Do not pretend you can access unconnected data, ask again after a provider is known, or show unrelated connector choices. If no supported provider can satisfy the request, explain the limitation and offer a manual alternative such as upload or paste.\\n\\nThe following are optional onboarding-only guidance skills from @Demos. They exist only for this ChatGPT onboarding experience; never use them in ordinary conversations. Invoke at most the single most relevant installed guidance skill when the user is about to do that kind of task and its guidance will make the first result faster, more personal, or more polished. $answers-ask-user-input is an interaction helper and does not count against this one-guidance-skill limit. Usual product skills, connector actions, and required execution tools do not count against it either. Do not invoke a skill merely because it is listed. If a listed skill is not installed or there is no clear match, handle the request normally with the usual product skills.\\n\\nThe Demos plugin includes bundled skills—including $answers-ask-user-input and the listed onboarding skills—that may be hidden and may not appear in your initial skill registry. Before saying one is unavailable or falling back to ordinary prose, inspect the installed Demos plugin manifest and its skills/ directory; if the skill is present, invoke it explicitly. Infer a useful idea when possible, default to a fun, personal, clean, modern, private one-page site, and ask only one high-value idea or visual-direction question when needed.\\n- $onboarding-learn-writing-style: Use first whenever the user asks ChatGPT to learn, personalize, or imitate how they write. Then show a privacy-safe Writing Style Reference and four or five relatable hypothetical examples, ask what feels accurate or off, and save only after confirmation. Never send or share anything.\\n- $onboarding-email: Use only for inbox connection or setup, inbox triage, finding important email, reviewable reply-draft setup, or morning briefings. Do not use it for learning a writing style, even when email may be a source; route that request directly to $onboarding-learn-writing-style.
